assert_distance_of_time_in_words(from, to=nil)

[ show source ]

    # File actionpack/test/template/date_helper_test.rb, line 21
21:   def assert_distance_of_time_in_words(from, to=nil)
22:     to ||= from
23: 
24:     # 0..1 with include_seconds
25:     assert_equal "less than 5 seconds", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 0.seconds, true)
26:     assert_equal "less than 5 seconds", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 4.seconds, true)
27:     assert_equal "less than 10 seconds", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 5.seconds, true)
28:     assert_equal "less than 10 seconds", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 9.seconds, true)
29:     assert_equal "less than 20 seconds", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 10.seconds, true)
30:     assert_equal "less than 20 seconds", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 19.seconds, true)
31:     assert_equal "half a minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 20.seconds, true)
32:     assert_equal "half a minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 39.seconds, true)
33:     assert_equal "less than a minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 40.seconds, true)
34:     assert_equal "less than a minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 59.seconds, true)
35:     assert_equal "1 minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 60.seconds, true)
36:     assert_equal "1 minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 89.seconds, true)
37: 
38:     # First case 0..1
39:     assert_equal "less than a minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 0.seconds)
40:     assert_equal "less than a minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 29.seconds)
41:     assert_equal "1 minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 30.seconds)
42:     assert_equal "1 minute", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 1.minutes + 29.seconds)
43: 
44:     # 2..44
45:     assert_equal "2 minutes", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 1.minutes + 30.seconds)
46:     assert_equal "44 minutes", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 44.minutes + 29.seconds)
47: 
48:     # 45..89
49:     assert_equal "about 1 hour", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 44.minutes + 30.seconds)
50:     assert_equal "about 1 hour", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 89.minutes + 29.seconds)
51: 
52:     # 90..1439
53:     assert_equal "about 2 hours", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 89.minutes + 30.seconds)
54:     assert_equal "about 24 hours", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 23.hours + 59.minutes + 29.seconds)
55: 
56:     # 1440..2529
57:     assert_equal "1 day", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 23.hours + 59.minutes + 30.seconds)
58:     assert_equal "1 day", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 41.hours + 59.minutes + 29.seconds)
59: 
60:     # 2530..43199
61:     assert_equal "2 days", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 42.hours + 59.minutes + 30.seconds)
62:     assert_equal "3 days", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 2.days + 12.hours)
63:     assert_equal "30 days", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 29.days + 23.hours + 59.minutes + 29.seconds)
64: 
65:     # 43200..86399
66:     assert_equal "about 1 month", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 29.days + 23.hours + 59.minutes + 30.seconds)
67:     assert_equal "about 1 month", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 59.days + 23.hours + 59.minutes + 29.seconds)
68: 
69:     # 86400..525599
70:     assert_equal "2 months", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 59.days + 23.hours + 59.minutes + 30.seconds)
71:     assert_equal "12 months", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 1.years - 31.seconds)
72: 
73:     # > 525599
74:     assert_equal "about 1 year",    distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 1.years - 30.seconds)
75:     assert_equal "about 1 year",    distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 1.years + 3.months - 1.day)
76:     assert_equal "over 1 year",     distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 1.years + 6.months)
77: 
78:     assert_equal "almost 2 years",  distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 2.years - 3.months + 1.day)
79:     assert_equal "about 2 years",   distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 2.years + 3.months - 1.day)
80:     assert_equal "over 2 years",    distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 2.years + 3.months + 1.day)
81:     assert_equal "over 2 years",    distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 2.years + 9.months - 1.day)
82:     assert_equal "almost 3 years",  distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 2.years + 9.months + 1.day)
83: 
84:     assert_equal "almost 5 years",  distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 5.years - 3.months + 1.day)
85:     assert_equal "about 5 years",   distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 5.years + 3.months - 1.day)
86:     assert_equal "over 5 years",    distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 5.years + 3.months + 1.day)
87:     assert_equal "over 5 years",    distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 5.years + 9.months - 1.day)
88:     assert_equal "almost 6 years",  distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 5.years + 9.months + 1.day)
89: 
90:     assert_equal "almost 10 years", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 10.years - 3.months + 1.day)
91:     assert_equal "about 10 years",  distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 10.years + 3.months - 1.day)
92:     assert_equal "over 10 years",   distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 10.years + 3.months + 1.day)
93:     assert_equal "over 10 years",   distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 10.years + 9.months - 1.day)
94:     assert_equal "almost 11 years", distance_of_time_in_words(from, to + 10.years + 9.months + 1.day)
95: 
96:     # test to < from
97:     assert_equal "about 4 hours", distance_of_time_in_words(from + 4.hours, to)
98:     assert_equal "less than 20 seconds", distance_of_time_in_words(from + 19.seconds, to, true)
99:   end

1195:   def test_date_select
1196:     @post = Post.new
1197:     @post.written_on = Date.new(2004, 6, 15)
1198: 
1199:     expected = %{<select id="post_written_on_1i" name="post[written_on(1i)]">\n}
1200:     expected << %{<option value="1999">1999</option>\n<option value="2000">2000</option>\n<option value="2001">2001</option>\n<option value="2002">2002</option>\n<option value="2003">2003</option>\n<option value="2004" selected="selected">2004</option>\n<option value="2005">2005</option>\n<option value="2006">2006</option>\n<option value="2007">2007</option>\n<option value="2008">2008</option>\n<option value="2009">2009</option>\n}
1201:     expected << "</select>\n"
1202: 
1203:     expected << %{<select id="post_written_on_2i" name="post[written_on(2i)]">\n}
1204:     expected << %{<option value="1">January</option>\n<option value="2">February</option>\n<option value="3">March</option>\n<option value="4">April</option>\n<option value="5">May</option>\n<option value="6" selected="selected">June</option>\n<option value="7">July</option>\n<option value="8">August</option>\n<option value="9">September</option>\n<option value="10">October</option>\n<option value="11">November</option>\n<option value="12">December</option>\n}
1205:     expected << "</select>\n"
1206: 
1207:     expected << %{<select id="post_written_on_3i" name="post[written_on(3i)]">\n}
1208:     expected << %{<option value="1">1</option>\n<option value="2">2</option>\n<option value="3">3</option>\n<option value="4">4</option>\n<option value="5">5</option>\n<option value="6">6</option>\n<option value="7">7</option>\n<option value="8">8</option>\n<option value="9">9</option>\n<option value="10">10</option>\n<option value="11">11</option>\n<option value="12">12</option>\n<option value="13">13</option>\n<option value="14">14</option>\n<option value="15" selected="selected">15</option>\n<option value="16">16</option>\n<option value="17">17</option>\n<option value="18">18</option>\n<option value="19">19</option>\n<option value="20">20</option>\n<option value="21">21</option>\n<option value="22">22</option>\n<option value="23">23</option>\n<option value="24">24</option>\n<option value="25">25</option>\n<option value="26">26</option>\n<option value="27">27</option>\n<option value="28">28</option>\n<option value="29">29</option>\n<option value="30">30</option>\n<option value="31">31</option>\n}
1209:

1421:   def test_date_select_cant_override_discard_hour
1422:     @post = Post.new
1423:     @post.written_on = Date.new(2004, 6, 15)
1424: 
1425:     expected = %{<select id="post_written_on_1i" name="post[written_on(1i)]">\n}
1426:     expected << %{<option value="1999">1999</option>\n<option value="2000">2000</option>\n<option value="2001">2001</option>\n<option value="2002">2002</option>\n<option value="2003">2003</option>\n<option value="2004" selected="selected">2004</option>\n<option value="2005">2005</option>\n<option value="2006">2006</option>\n<option value="2007">2007</option>\n<option value="2008">2008</option>\n<option value="2009">2009</option>\n}
1427:     expected << "</select>\n"
1428: 
1429:     expected << %{<select id="post_written_on_2i" name="post[written_on(2i)]">\n}
1430:     expected << %{<option value="1">January</option>\n<option value="2">February</option>\n<option value="3">March</option>\n<option value="4">April</option>\n<option value="5">May</option>\n<option value="6" selected="selected">June</option>\n<option value="7">July</option>\n<option value="8">August</option>\n<option value="9">September</option>\n<option value="10">October</option>\n<option value="11">November</option>\n<option value="12">December</option>\n}
1431:     expected << "</select>\n"
1432: 
1433:     expected << %{<select id="post_written_on_3i" name="post[written_on(3i)]">\n}
1434:     expected << %{<option value="1">1</option>\n<option value="2">2</option>\n<option value="3">3</option>\n<option value="4">4</option>\n<option value="5">5</option>\n<option value="6">6</option>\n<option value="7">7</option>\n<option value="8">8</option>\n<option value="9">9</option>\n<option value="10">10</option>\n<option value="11">11</option>\n<option value="12">12</option>\n<option value="13">13</option>\n<option value="14">14</option>\n<option value="15" selected="selected">15</option>\n<option value="16">16</option>\n<option value="17">17</option>\n<option value="18">18</option>\n<option value="19">19</option>\n<option value="20">20</option>\n<option value="21">21</option>\n<option value="22">22</option>\n<option value="23">23</option>\n<option value="24">24</option>\n<option value="25">25</option>\n<option value="26">26</option>\n<option value="27">27</option>\n<option value="28">28</option>\n<option value="29">29</option>\n<option value="30">30</option>\n<option value="31">31</option>\n}
1435:     expected << "</select>\n"
1436: 
1437:     assert_dom_equal expected, date_select("post", "written_on", :discard_hour => false)
1438:   end
test_date_select_should_not_change_passed_options_hash()

[ show source ]

      # File actionpack/test/template/date_helper_test.rb, line 2331
2331:   def test_date_select_should_not_change_passed_options_hash
2332:     @post = Post.new
2333:     @post.updated_at = Time.local(2008, 7, 16, 23, 30)
2334: 
2335:     options = {
2336:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2337:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2338:       :discard_type => false,
2339:       :include_blank => false,
2340:       :ignore_date => false,
2341:       :include_seconds => true
2342:     }
2343:     date_select(@post, :updated_at, options)
2344: 
2345:     # note: the literal hash is intentional to show that the actual options hash isn't modified
2346:     #       don't change this!
2347:     assert_equal({
2348:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2349:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2350:       :discard_type => false,
2351:       :include_blank => false,
2352:       :ignore_date => false,
2353:       :include_seconds => true
2354:     }, options)
2355:   end

test_datetime_select_discard_month()

[ show source ]

      # File actionpack/test/template/date_helper_test.rb, line 2134
2134:   def test_datetime_select_discard_month
2135:     @post = Post.new
2136:     @post.updated_at = Time.local(2004, 6, 15, 15, 16, 35)
2137: 
2138:     expected = %{<select id="post_updated_at_1i" name="post[updated_at(1i)]">\n}
2139:     1999.upto(2009) { |i| expected << %(<option value="#{i}"#{' selected="selected"' if i == 2004}>#{i}</option>\n) }
2140:     expected << "</select>\n"
2141:     expected << %{<input type="hidden" id="post_updated_at_2i" name="post[updated_at(2i)]" value="6" />\n}
2142:     expected << %{<input type="hidden" id="post_updated_at_3i" name="post[updated_at(3i)]" value="15" />\n}
2143: 
2144:     expected << " &mdash; "
2145: 
2146:     expected << %{<select id="post_updated_at_4i" name="post[updated_at(4i)]">\n}
2147:     0.upto(23) { |i| expected << %(<option value="#{sprintf("%02d", i)}"#{' selected="selected"' if i == 15}>#{sprintf("%02d", i)}</option>\n) }
2148:     expected << "</select>\n"
2149:     expected << " : "
2150:     expected << %{<select id="post_updated_at_5i" name="post[updated_at(5i)]">\n}
2151:     0.upto(59) { |i| expected << %(<option value="#{sprintf("%02d", i)}"#{' selected="selected"' if i == 16}>#{sprintf("%02d", i)}</option>\n) }
2152:     expected << "</select>\n"
2153: 
2154:     assert_dom_equal expected, datetime_select("post", "updated_at", :discard_month => true)
2155:   end

test_datetime_select_should_not_change_passed_options_hash()

[ show source ]

      # File actionpack/test/template/date_helper_test.rb, line 2357
2357:   def test_datetime_select_should_not_change_passed_options_hash
2358:     @post = Post.new
2359:     @post.updated_at = Time.local(2008, 7, 16, 23, 30)
2360: 
2361:     options = {
2362:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2363:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2364:       :discard_type => false,
2365:       :include_blank => false,
2366:       :ignore_date => false,
2367:       :include_seconds => true
2368:     }
2369:     datetime_select(@post, :updated_at, options)
2370: 
2371:     # note: the literal hash is intentional to show that the actual options hash isn't modified
2372:     #       don't change this!
2373:     assert_equal({
2374:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2375:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2376:       :discard_type => false,
2377:       :include_blank => false,
2378:       :ignore_date => false,
2379:       :include_seconds => true
2380:     }, options)
2381:   end

test_select_datetime_should_not_change_passed_options_hash()

      # File actionpack/test/template/date_helper_test.rb, line 2432
2432:   def test_select_datetime_should_not_change_passed_options_hash
2433:     options = {
2434:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2435:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2436:       :discard_type => false,
2437:       :include_blank => false,
2438:       :ignore_date => false,
2439:       :include_seconds => true
2440:     }
2441:     select_datetime(Time.now, options)
2442: 
2443:     # note: the literal hash is intentional to show that the actual options hash isn't modified
2444:     #       don't change this!
2445:     assert_equal({
2446:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2447:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2448:       :discard_type => false,
2449:       :include_blank => false,
2450:       :ignore_date => false,
2451:       :include_seconds => true
2452:     }, options)
2453:   end

      # File actionpack/test/template/date_helper_test.rb, line 2455
2455:   def test_select_time_should_not_change_passed_options_hash
2456:     options = {
2457:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2458:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2459:       :discard_type => false,
2460:       :include_blank => false,
2461:       :ignore_date => false,
2462:       :include_seconds => true
2463:     }
2464:     select_time(Time.now, options)
2465: 
2466:     # note: the literal hash is intentional to show that the actual options hash isn't modified
2467:     #       don't change this!
2468:     assert_equal({
2469:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2470:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2471:       :discard_type => false,
2472:       :include_blank => false,
2473:       :ignore_date => false,
2474:       :include_seconds => true
2475:     }, options)
2476:   end

1551:

1553:     expected << %{<input type="hidden" id="post_written_on_2i" name="post[written_on(2i)]" value="6" />\n}

1555:

1563:

1565:   end
test_time_select_should_not_change_passed_options_hash()

[ show source ]

      # File actionpack/test/template/date_helper_test.rb, line 2383
2383:   def test_time_select_should_not_change_passed_options_hash
2384:     @post = Post.new
2385:     @post.updated_at = Time.local(2008, 7, 16, 23, 30)
2386: 
2387:     options = {
2388:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2389:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2390:       :discard_type => false,
2391:       :include_blank => false,
2392:       :ignore_date => false,
2393:       :include_seconds => true
2394:     }
2395:     time_select(@post, :updated_at, options)
2396: 
2397:     # note: the literal hash is intentional to show that the actual options hash isn't modified
2398:     #       don't change this!
2399:     assert_equal({
2400:       :order => [ :year, :month, :day ],
2401:       :default => { :year => 2008, :month => 7, :day => 16, :hour => 23, :minute => 30, :second => 1 },
2402:       :discard_type => false,
2403:       :include_blank => false,
2404:       :ignore_date => false,
2405:       :include_seconds => true
2406:     }, options)
2407:   end

test_time_select_with_html_options_within_fields_for()

[ show source ]

      # File actionpack/test/template/date_helper_test.rb, line 1624
1624:   def test_time_select_with_html_options_within_fields_for
1625:     @post = Post.new
1626:     @post.written_on = Time.local(2004, 6, 15, 15, 16, 35)
1627: 
1628:     fields_for :post, @post do |f|
1629:       concat f.time_select(:written_on, {}, :class => 'selector')
1630:     end
1631: 
1632:     expected = %{<input type="hidden" id="post_written_on_1i" name="post[written_on(1i)]" value="2004" />\n}
1633:     expected << %{<input type="hidden" id="post_written_on_2i" name="post[written_on(2i)]" value="6" />\n}
1634:     expected << %{<input type="hidden" id="post_written_on_3i" name="post[written_on(3i)]" value="15" />\n}
1635: 
1636:     expected << %(<select id="post_written_on_4i" name="post[written_on(4i)]" class="selector">\n)
1637:     0.upto(23) { |i| expected << %(<option value="#{sprintf("%02d", i)}"#{' selected="selected"' if i == 15}>#{sprintf("%02d", i)}</option>\n) }
1638:     expected << "</select>\n"
1639:     expected << " : "
1640:     expected << %(<select id="post_written_on_5i" name="post[written_on(5i)]" class="selector">\n)
1641:     0.upto(59) { |i| expected << %(<option value="#{sprintf("%02d", i)}"#{' selected="selected"' if i == 16}>#{sprintf("%02d", i)}</option>\n) }
1642:     expected << "</select>\n"
